);

#Nitesh Kumar 9th Nov 2017
delimiter //
DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS getVendorInvoiceGSTTerms;
CREATE FUNCTION getVendorInvoiceGSTTerms(grdetailsid varchar(255)) returns varchar(255)
begin
declare gstamount varchar(255);
set gstamount= '';
select GROUP_CONCAT(linelevelterms.term,':',receiptdetailtermsmap.termamount SEPARATOR ',')  into gstamount from receiptdetailtermsmap LEFT JOIN linelevelterms ON receiptdetailtermsmap.term = linelevelterms.id where receiptdetailtermsmap.goodsreceiptdetail=grdetailsid and linelevelterms.salesorpurchase=0;
return gstamount;
end//
delimiter ;


delimiter //
DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS getInvoiceGSTTerms;
CREATE FUNCTION getInvoiceGSTTerms(invoicedetailid varchar(255)) returns varchar(255)
begin
declare gstamount varchar(255);
set gstamount= '';
select GROUP_CONCAT(linelevelterms.term,':',invoicedetailtermsmap.termamount SEPARATOR ',')  into gstamount from invoicedetailtermsmap LEFT JOIN linelevelterms ON invoicedetailtermsmap.term = linelevelterms.id where invoicedetailtermsmap.invoicedetail=invoicedetailid and linelevelterms.salesorpurchase=1;
return gstamount;
end//
delimiter ;

delimiter //
DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS getSalesreturnGSTTerms;
CREATE FUNCTION getSalesreturnGSTTerms(srdetailsid varchar(255)) returns varchar(255)
begin
declare gstamount varchar(255);
set gstamount= '';
select GROUP_CONCAT(linelevelterms.term,':',salesreturndetailtermmap.termamount SEPARATOR ',')  into gstamount from salesreturndetailtermmap LEFT JOIN linelevelterms ON salesreturndetailtermmap.term = linelevelterms.id where salesreturndetailtermmap.salesreturndetail=srdetailsid and linelevelterms.salesorpurchase=1;
return gstamount;
end//
delimiter ;

delimiter //
DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS getPurchasereturnGSTTerms;
CREATE FUNCTION getPurchasereturnGSTTerms(prdetailsid varchar(255)) returns varchar(255)
begin
declare gstamount varchar(255);
set gstamount= '';
select GROUP_CONCAT(linelevelterms.term,':',purchasereturndetailtermmap.termamount SEPARATOR ',')  into gstamount from purchasereturndetailtermmap LEFT JOIN linelevelterms ON purchasereturndetailtermmap.term = linelevelterms.id where purchasereturndetailtermmap.purchasereturndetail=prdetailsid and linelevelterms.salesorpurchase=0;
return gstamount;
end//
delimiter ;

  `id` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  `defaultheaderid` VARCHAR(255) NULL,
  `defaulttermsid` VARCHAR(255) NULL, 
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreportsgstfieldslineleveltermsmapping_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`defaulttermsid`) REFERENCES `linelevelterms` (`defaultterms`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `purchaseorderversion` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `ponumber` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `autogen` char(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `orderdate` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `duedate` date DEFAULT NULL,

  `deleteflag` char(1) NOT NULL,

  `costcenter` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,

  `linkedsoblocked` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',

	`version` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,

  KEY `FK_B1F87AED8B3E9C77` (`vendor`),
  KEY `FK_B1F87AED7E350577` (`company`),
  KEY `FK_B1F87AED731A0B77` (`tax`),

  KEY `FK_poversioncurrency` (`currency`),
  KEY `FK_ApproverForbillingpoversion` (`approver`),

  KEY `FK_jobworklocation` (`jobworklocation`),

  CONSTRAINT `FK_B1F87AED731A0B77` FOREIGN KEY (`tax`) REFERENCES `tax` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_B1F87AED7E350577` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_B1F87AED8B3E9C77` FOREIGN KEY (`vendor`) REFERENCES `vendor` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_CF1EA548D06BCCC` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `creditterm` (`termid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_billingshippingaddresses_poversion` FOREIGN KEY (`billingshippingaddresses`) REFERENCES `billingshippingaddresses` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_poversion_seqformat` FOREIGN KEY (`seqformat`) REFERENCES `sequenceformat` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_poversioncurrency` FOREIGN KEY (`currency`) REFERENCES `currency` (`currencyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `poversion_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`createdby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `poversion_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`modifiedby`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `poversion_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`masteragent`) REFERENCES `masteritem` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `poversion_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `poversion_ibfk_5` FOREIGN KEY (`jobworklocation`) REFERENCES `inventorylocation` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `povdetails` varchar(225) NOT NULL,
  `product` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` double DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `creator` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `purchasevalueorsalevalue` double DEFAULT '0',
  `deductionorabatementpercent` double DEFAULT '0',
  `taxtype` int(1) DEFAULT '1',
  `assessablevalue` double DEFAULT '0',
  `isgstapplied` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `entityterm` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_1` (`term`),
  KEY `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_2` (`povdetails`),
  KEY `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_3` (`product`),
  KEY `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_entityterm` (`entityterm`),
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `linelevelterms` (`id`) ,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`povdetails`) REFERENCES `poversiondetails` (`id`) ,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_3` FOREIGN KEY (`product`) REFERENCES `product` (`id`) ,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderversiondetailstermmap_ibfk_4` FOREIGN KEY (`entityterm`) REFERENCES `entitybasedlineleveltermsrate` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE `purchaseorderversiontermmap` (
  `id` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `term` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `purchaseorderversion` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `termamount` double DEFAULT '0',
  `percentage` double DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(4) DEFAULT '0',

  `createdon` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `purchaseorderversiontermmap_ibfk_1` (`term`),
  KEY `purchaseorderversiontermmap_ibfk_2` (`purchaseorderversion`),
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderversiontermmap_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`term`) REFERENCES `invoicetermssales` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `purchaseorderversiontermmap_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`purchaseorderversion`) REFERENCES `purchaseorderversion` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

CREATE TABLE integrationdetails (
  id VARCHAR (255) NOT NULL,
  company VARCHAR (255) NOT NULL,
  integrationpartyid SMALLINT NOT NULL,
  username VARCHAR (63),
  passkey VARCHAR(63),
  licensekey VARCHAR(63),
  accountnumber VARCHAR(63),
  restserviceurl VARCHAR(255),
  configjson TEXT,
  PRIMARY KEY (id),
  FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company (companyid)
) ENGINE = INNODB DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8;

	parentrecordid VARCHAR (63) NOT NULL,
	avalarataxdetails text,
	PRIMARY KEY (parentrecordid)
) ENGINE = INNODB DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8;

  productid VARCHAR (63) NOT NULL,
  avalaraitemid  VARCHAR (63) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (productid),
  FOREIGN KEY (productid) REFERENCES product (id) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE = INNODB DEFAULT CHARSET = utf8;

#Swapnesh Kulkarni 28th Nov 2017
update fieldcombodata fcd1 inner join (select fcd.id,fcd.value,state.rowNumber from fieldcombodata fcd inner join fieldparams fp on fp.id=fcd.fieldid inner join (SELECT (@cnt := @cnt + 1) AS rowNumber, t.*  FROM defaultstatevalues AS t CROSS JOIN (SELECT @cnt := 0) AS dummy ORDER BY t.statename) state on fcd.value=state.statename where fp.fieldname='custom_state' and fp.companyid in(select companyid from company where country=105)) temp on fcd1.id=temp.id set itemsequence = temp.rowNumber;
